<span class="expr-badge">Thermosynechococcus vulcanus</span>

## Overview

The [Photosystem II](/xray-mp-wiki/proteins/photosynthesis/photosystem-ii/) (PSII) core dimer from the thermophilic cyanobacterium Thermosynechococcus elongatus has been solved at multiple resolutions by X-ray crystallography. The 3.5 A structure (PDB 1S5L) revealed a homodimer with the membrane integral part measuring 190 A x 100 A and 40 A thick. Time-resolved [Serial Femtosecond Crystallography](/xray-mp-wiki/methods/structure-determination/serial-femtosecond-crystallography/) ([TR-SFX](/xray-mp-wiki/methods/structure-determination/time-resolved-serial-femtosecond-crystallography/)) structures have been determined at 5 A (dark S1 state, PDB 4PBU) and 5.5 A (double-flash putative S3 state, PDB 4Q54), revealing significant conformational changes at the oxygen-evolving complex and electron acceptor side during the [Kok Cycle](/xray-mp-wiki/concepts/enzyme-mechanisms/kok-cycle/) of water oxidation.

      <td>PSII core dimer from Thermosynechococcus elongatus, comprising D1, D2, CP43, CP47, cytochrome b-559 (alpha and beta), PsbI, PsbX, PsbH, PsbK, PsbL, and extrinsic proteins PsbO, PsbV, PsbU, and cytochrome c-550</td>
      <td>Chlorophyll a, pheophytin a, <a href="/xray-mp-wiki/reagents/ligands/heme/">HEME</a>, non-<a href="/xray-mp-wiki/reagents/ligands/heme/">HEME</a> <a href="/xray-mp-wiki/reagents/additives/iron/">IRON</a>, Mn4CaO5 manganese cluster, <a href="/xray-mp-wiki/reagents/ligands/plastoquinone/">Plastoquinone</a>, bicarbonate, carotenoids</td>
    </tr>
  </tbody>
</table>

**Expression:**

- **Expression system**: Thermosynechococcus elongatus (thermophilic cyanobacterium)
- **Construct**: PSII core dimer from wild-type strain

**Crystallization:**

<table class="wiki-kv-table">
  <tbody>
    <tr>
      <td>Method</td>
      <td>Crystallography of PSII crystals</td>
    </tr>
    <tr>
      <td>Protein sample</td>
      <td>PSII core dimer from T. elongatus</td>
    </tr>
    <tr>
      <td>Notes</td>
      <td>Crystals were grown and cryocooled for X-ray diffraction. The structure was solved using multiple heavy atom derivatives including <a href="/xray-mp-wiki/reagents/additives/cadmium-chloride/">Cadmium Chloride</a>, <a href="/xray-mp-wiki/reagents/additives/mercury/">Mercury (HgCl2) - Aquaporin Inhibitor</a> compounds, gold chloride, and platinum chloride for SAD/MAD phasing. The best native dataset diffracted to 3.5 A resolution with space group P212121. The dimer has a local-C2 rotation axis perpendicular to the membrane plane. The pseudo-C2 axis within each monomer is parallel to the local-C2 axis and passes through the non-<a href="/xray-mp-wiki/reagents/ligands/heme/">HEME</a> <a href="/xray-mp-wiki/reagents/additives/iron/">IRON</a> at the stromal side.
</td>
    </tr>
  </tbody>
</table>

### doi/10.1038##nature13453

**Structures:**

<table class="wiki-table">
  <thead><tr>
    <th>PDB ID</th>
    <th>Resolution</th>
    <th>Space Group</th>
    <th>Construct</th>
    <th>Ligand/Co-factor</th>
  </tr></thead>
  <tbody>
    <tr>
      <td><a class="pdb-link" href="https://www.rcsb.org/structure/4pbu">4PBU</a></td>
      <td>5.0</td>
      <td>P212121</td>
      <td>PSII core dimer from Thermosynechococcus elongatus, dark S1 state, <a href="/xray-mp-wiki/methods/structure-determination/serial-femtosecond-crystallography/">Serial Femtosecond Crystallography</a></td>
      <td>Chlorophyll a, beta-carotene, pheophytin a, <a href="/xray-mp-wiki/reagents/ligands/plastoquinone/">Plastoquinone</a> (QA, QB), haem, bicarbonate, lipids, Mn4CaO5 cluster, non-haem <a href="/xray-mp-wiki/reagents/additives/iron/">IRON</a>, Ca2+</td>
    </tr>
    <tr>
      <td><a class="pdb-link" href="https://www.rcsb.org/structure/4q54">4Q54</a></td>
      <td>5.5</td>
      <td>P212121</td>
      <td>PSII core dimer from Thermosynechococcus elongatus, double-flash putative S3 state, <a href="/xray-mp-wiki/methods/structure-determination/serial-femtosecond-crystallography/">Serial Femtosecond Crystallography</a></td>
      <td>Chlorophyll a, beta-carotene, pheophytin a, <a href="/xray-mp-wiki/reagents/ligands/plastoquinone/">Plastoquinone</a> (QA, QB), haem, bicarbonate, lipids, Mn4CaO5 cluster, non-haem <a href="/xray-mp-wiki/reagents/additives/iron/">IRON</a>, Ca2+</td>
    </tr>
  </tbody>
</table>

**Expression:**

- **Expression system**: Thermosynechococcus elongatus (thermophilic cyanobacterium)
- **Construct**: PSII core dimer from wild-type strain

**Crystallization:**

<table class="wiki-kv-table">
  <tbody>
    <tr>
      <td>Method</td>
      <td><a href="/xray-mp-wiki/methods/crystallization/batch-crystallization-free-interface-diffusion/">Batch Crystallization with Free Interface Diffusion</a></td>
    </tr>
    <tr>
      <td>Protein sample</td>
      <td>PSII core complex in solubilization buffer: 100 mM PIPES pH 7.0, 5 mM CaCl2, 10 mM <a href="/xray-mp-wiki/reagents/additives/tocopherol/">Tocopherol (Vitamin E)</a>, 0.03% beta-dodecylmaltsyl (<a href="/xray-mp-wiki/reagents/detergents/ddm/">DDM</a>)</td>
    </tr>
    <tr>
      <td>Temperature</td>
      <td>10 °C</td>
    </tr>
    <tr>
      <td>Growth time</td>
      <td>48 hours</td>
    </tr>
    <tr>
      <td>Cryoprotection</td>
      <td>Not specified; crystals delivered at 10 °C via gas focusing liquid injector</td>
    </tr>
    <tr>
      <td>Notes</td>
      <td>PSII nano/microcrystals (~1 um) grown by free interface diffusion enhanced sedimentation method for <a href="/xray-mp-wiki/methods/structure-determination/time-resolved-serial-femtosecond-crystallography/">TR-SFX</a> at LCLS. Dark S1 state (PDB 4PBU, 5 A) and double-flash putative S3 state (PDB 4Q54, 5.5 A) data collected at FEL frequency of 120 Hz with alternating dark and double-flash patterns. Unit cell dimensions: dark S1 a=133 A, b=226 A, c=307 A; S3 state a=137 A, b=228 A, c=309 A. Data phased by <a href="/xray-mp-wiki/methods/structure-determination/molecular-replacement/">Molecular Replacement</a> using PDB 3ARC.</td>
    </tr>
  </tbody>
</table>

      <td>PSII core dimer from Thermosynechococcus elongatus, room temperature dark-adapted S1 state, <a href="/xray-mp-wiki/methods/structure-determination/serial-femtosecond-crystallography/">Serial Femtosecond Crystallography</a> at LCLS</td>
      <td>Chlorophyll a, beta-carotene, pheophytin a, <a href="/xray-mp-wiki/reagents/ligands/plastoquinone/">Plastoquinone</a> (QA, QB), haem, bicarbonate, Mn4CaO5 cluster, non-haem <a href="/xray-mp-wiki/reagents/additives/iron/">IRON</a>, Cl-</td>
    </tr>
    <tr>
      <td><a class="pdb-link" href="https://www.rcsb.org/structure/5kaf">5KAF</a></td>
      <td>2.35</td>
      <td>P212121</td>
      <td>PSII core dimer from Thermosynechococcus elongatus, room temperature two-flash illuminated S3-enriched state, <a href="/xray-mp-wiki/methods/structure-determination/serial-femtosecond-crystallography/">Serial Femtosecond Crystallography</a> at LCLS</td>
      <td>Chlorophyll a, beta-carotene, pheophytin a, <a href="/xray-mp-wiki/reagents/ligands/plastoquinone/">Plastoquinone</a> (QA, QB), haem, bicarbonate, Mn4CaO5 cluster, non-haem <a href="/xray-mp-wiki/reagents/additives/iron/">IRON</a>, Cl-</td>
    </tr>

      <td><a class="pdb-link" href="https://www.rcsb.org/structure/5kaf">5KAF</a></td>
      <td>2.8</td>
      <td>P212121</td>
      <td>PSII core dimer from Thermosynechococcus elongatus, room temperature two-flash illuminated S3-enriched state with 100 mM (NH4)2SO4, <a href="/xray-mp-wiki/methods/structure-determination/serial-femtosecond-crystallography/">Serial Femtosecond Crystallography</a> at LCLS</td>
      <td>Chlorophyll a, beta-carotene, pheophytin a, <a href="/xray-mp-wiki/reagents/ligands/plastoquinone/">Plastoquinone</a> (QA, QB), haem, bicarbonate, Mn4CaO5 cluster, non-haem <a href="/xray-mp-wiki/reagents/additives/iron/">IRON</a>, Cl-</td>
    </tr>
  </tbody>
</table>

**Expression:**

- **Expression system**: Thermosynechococcus elongatus (thermophilic cyanobacterium)
- **Construct**: PSII core dimer from wild-type strain

**Crystallization:**

<table class="wiki-kv-table">
  <tbody>
    <tr>
      <td>Method</td>
      <td>Batch crystallization with microseeding</td>
    </tr>
    <tr>
      <td>Protein sample</td>
      <td>PSII core complex in 100 mM TRIS-Cl pH 7.5, 100 mM (NH4)2SO4, 31.5% <a href="/xray-mp-wiki/reagents/additives/peg/">PEG</a> 5000, 10% <a href="/xray-mp-wiki/reagents/additives/ethylene-glycol/">Ethylene Glycol</a> (CXI); or 100 mM MES pH 6.5, 100 mM NH4Cl, 10% <a href="/xray-mp-wiki/reagents/additives/ethylene-glycol/">Ethylene Glycol</a>, 35% <a href="/xray-mp-wiki/reagents/additives/peg/">PEG</a> 5000 (XPP/MFX)</td>
    </tr>
    <tr>
      <td>Temperature</td>
      <td>Room temperature</td>
    </tr>
    <tr>
      <td>Growth time</td>
      <td>Variable (crystals 5-15 um or 20-50 um)</td>
    </tr>
    <tr>
      <td>Cryoprotection</td>
      <td>10% <a href="/xray-mp-wiki/reagents/additives/ethylene-glycol/">Ethylene Glycol</a>, high <a href="/xray-mp-wiki/reagents/additives/peg/">PEG</a> 5000 (dehydration)</td>
    </tr>
    <tr>
      <td>Notes</td>
      <td>PSII crystals grown with microseeding for uniform size distribution. Two crystal forms: CXI data (MESH injector, 5-15 um crystals) and XPP/MFX data (ADE-DOT injector, 20-50 um crystals). Unit cell: a=118.2 A, b=224.6 A, c=331.9 A, similar to Hellmich packing. Crystal dehydration with high <a href="/xray-mp-wiki/reagents/additives/peg/">PEG</a> 5000 resulted in ordered room temperature diffraction. Data collected at LCLS with femtosecond XFEL pulses to obtain damage-free structures at room temperature.</td>
    </tr>
  </tbody>
</table>

## Biological / Functional Insights

### D1/D2 reaction center architecture

The D1 and D2 subunits form the reaction center core with each containing five transmembrane alpha-helices arranged in two semicircles interlocked in a handshake motif related by the pseudo-C2 axis. The alpha-helices C and D of each subunit are connected by a long alpha-helix CD on the luminal side. The short alpha-helix DE on the stromal side connects alpha-helices D and E. Subunits D1 and D2 are distinguished by the position of the manganese cluster, which is coordinated by D1, and the QA binding site, which is located at D2. The arrangement of alpha-helices of D1 and D2 resembles that of subunits L and M in the purple bacterial reaction centre.

### Inner antenna organization (CP43 and CP47)

CP43 and CP47 are inner antenna subunits that flank both sides of the D1/D2/cytochrome b-559 complex. CP43 contains 12 chlorophyll a molecules and CP47 contains 14 chlorophyll a molecules, totaling 26 chlorophyll a in the core dimer. Both subunits consist of six transmembrane alpha-helices arranged as a trimer of dimers related by the pseudo-C2 axis. The center-to-center distances between pairs of nearest chlorophylls range from 8.5 to 13.5 A. The chlorophyll a molecules occupy two layers close to the stromal and luminal sides of the membrane.

### Electron transfer chain symmetry

The cofactors of the electron transfer chain form two branches organized symmetrically along the pseudo-C2 axis, assigned to the D1 and D2 proteins by analogy with the purple bacterial reaction centre. Towards the luminal side, two chlorophyll a molecules PD1 and PD2 are observed with a Mg-Mg distance of 10 A and parallel head groups with 5 A interplanar distance. The symmetric arrangement supports the hypothesis that all photosynthetic reaction centres evolved from a common ancestor.

### Extrinsic proteins on the luminal side

Three extrinsic subunits are located on the luminal side of PSII: the manganese-stabilizing 33K protein (PsbO), the 17K protein (PsbV), and the 12K protein (PsbU). Cytochrome c-550 is also located on the luminal side, identified by its haem [IRON](/xray-mp-wiki/reagents/additives/iron/). The PsbO subunit forms a roughly 35 A long cylindrical arrangement of beta-strands tilted 45 degrees against the membrane. The 12K subunit (PsbU) was not unambiguously located in the electron density map due to unassigned secondary structure elements.

### Time-resolved conformational changes in the S-state cycle

[TR-SFX](/xray-mp-wiki/methods/structure-determination/time-resolved-serial-femtosecond-crystallography/) structures of PSII in the dark S1 state (PDB 4PBU, 5 A) and double-flash putative S3 state (PDB 4Q54, 5.5 A) reveal significant conformational changes. The Mn4CaO5 cluster elongates in the S3 state with increased distance between the Mn3CaOx cubane and the dangler Mn (Mn4), potentially allowing binding of the second substrate water molecule. At the acceptor side, changes in electron density at the loop regions and the position of the non-haem [IRON](/xray-mp-wiki/reagents/additives/iron/) are observed. The CD loop (including D170) may move away from the cluster while the AB loop (with D61) moves closer. Unit cell dimensions increase upon double-flash excitation (a: 133 to 137 A), and these changes reverse upon triple-flash reaching putative S4 state.

### Room temperature XFEL structures reveal damage-free PSII at S1 and S3 states

Using femtosecond XFEL pulses from LCLS, room temperature structures of PSII were obtained in the dark-adapted S1 state (PDB 5GTH, 2.35 A), two-flash illuminated S3-enriched state (PDB 5GTI, 2.35 A), and ammonia-bound S3-enriched state (PDB 5GTJ, 2.8 A). The room temperature structures show a 0.5-0.6 A shift in TMH2 of CP47 compared to cryogenic structures, attributed to thermal expansion rather than crystal packing. Cofactor-cofactor distances in the electron transport chain are generally elongated at room temperature compared to cryogenic conditions, particularly involving ChlZ and QB-Cyt b-559 distances.

### Substrate water binding probed by ammonia competition in S3 state

Ammonia binding experiments in the S3-enriched state identify the terminal water ligands on Mn4 (W1, W2) as candidate substrate binding sites. Ammonia does not affect substrate water exchange rates in S2 and S3 states, suggesting that W2 is unlikely to be a substrate binding site in the S3 state. This disfavors O-O bond formation via nucleophilic attack from Ca-bound W3 onto W2. The data support alternative mechanisms including oxo-oxyl radical coupling between a hydroxo on Mn1 and O5, or nucleophilic attack of W3 onto O5.

### Minimal structural changes in OEC between S1 and S3 states

Small movements on the order of 0.3 A are observed in side chains surrounding the Mn4CaO5 cluster upon S2 to S3 transition, with no large conformational changes of D1 residues Asp61, Asp170, or Val185. The Mn3-Mn4 distance does not elongate in the S3 state, ruling out di-mu-oxo to mono-mu-oxo bridge conversion. No additional water or hydroxo ligand was observed near Mn1 in the S3 state, arguing against water insertion at that specific position.

- <a href="/xray-mp-wiki/reagents/additives/cadmium-chloride/">Cadmium Chloride</a> — Heavy atom derivative used for SAD phasing of PSII crystals

- <a href="/xray-mp-wiki/methods/structure-determination/time-resolved-serial-femtosecond-crystallography/">Time-Resolved Serial Femtosecond Crystallography</a> — TR-SFX technique enabled time-resolved study of S-state transitions in PSII
